<p><i><b>The SpongeBob SquarePants Movie</b></i> is a 2004 American <a href="/wiki/Animation" title="Animation">animated</a> <a href="/wiki/Adventure_film" title="Adventure film">adventure</a> <a href="/wiki/Comedy_film" title="Comedy film">comedy film</a> based on the <a href="/wiki/Nickelodeon" title="Nickelodeon">Nickelodeon</a> <a href="/wiki/SpongeBob_SquarePants" title="SpongeBob SquarePants">television series of the same name</a>. The film was directed by series creator <a href="/wiki/Stephen_Hillenburg" title="Stephen Hillenburg">Stephen Hillenburg</a> and starred the series' cast of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Kenny" title="Tom Kenny">Tom Kenny</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bill_Fagerbakke" title="Bill Fagerbakke">Bill Fagerbakke</a>, <a href="/wiki/Clancy_Brown" title="Clancy Brown">Clancy Brown</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rodger_Bumpass" title="Rodger Bumpass">Rodger Bumpass</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mr._Lawrence" title="Mr. Lawrence">Mr. Lawrence</a>, with guest performances by <a href="/wiki/Scarlett_Johansson" title="Scarlett Johansson">Scarlett Johansson</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jeffrey_Tambor" title="Jeffrey Tambor">Jeffrey Tambor</a>, <a href="/wiki/Alec_Baldwin" title="Alec Baldwin">Alec Baldwin</a> and <a href="/wiki/David_Hasselhoff" title="David Hasselhoff">David Hasselhoff</a>. It was produced by Hillenburg's production company <a href="/wiki/United_Plankton_Pictures" title="United Plankton Pictures">United Plankton Pictures</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nickelodeon_Movies" title="Nickelodeon Movies">Nickelodeon Movies</a> and was distributed by <a href="/wiki/Paramount_Pictures" title="Paramount Pictures">Paramount Pictures</a>. In the film, <a href="/wiki/Plankton_(character)" title="Plankton (character)">Plankton</a> devises a plan to steal <a href="/wiki/Neptune_(mythology)" title="Neptune (mythology)">King Neptune</a>'s crown and send it to Shell City, and <a href="/wiki/SpongeBob_SquarePants_(character)" title="SpongeBob SquarePants (character)">SpongeBob</a> and <a href="/wiki/Patrick_Star" title="Patrick Star">Patrick</a> must retrieve the crown to save <a href="/wiki/Mr._Krabs" title="Mr. Krabs">Mr. Krabs</a> from King Neptune's wrath and Bikini Bottom from Plankton's plan.</p>
<p>Previous offers by Paramount Pictures for a film adaptation of <i>SpongeBob SquarePants</i> had been rejected by Stephen Hillenburg, but he eventually accepted one offer in 2002. A writing team consisting of Hillenburg, <a href="/wiki/Paul_Tibbitt" title="Paul Tibbitt">Paul Tibbitt</a>, <a href="/wiki/Derek_Drymon" title="Derek Drymon">Derek Drymon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Aaron_Springer" title="Aaron Springer">Aaron Springer</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kent_Osborne" title="Kent Osborne">Kent Osborne</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tim_Hill_(director)" title="Tim Hill (director)">Tim Hill</a> was assembled, conceiving the idea of a mythical hero's quest and the search for a stolen crown, which would bring SpongeBob and Patrick to the surface. The film was originally intended as the <a href="/wiki/Series_finale" title="Series finale">series finale</a>, but Nickelodeon ordered more episodes of the series after the film's success, so Hillenburg resigned as Showrunner, with Tibbitt taking Hillenburg's Place.</p>
<p>The film was promoted immensely by Paramount and Nickelodeon, with tie-in promotions made by <a href="/wiki/7-Eleven" title="7-Eleven">7-Eleven</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Cayman_Islands" title="Cayman Islands">Cayman Islands</a> and <a href="/wiki/Burger_King" title="Burger King">Burger King</a>, which decorated various of its franchises with 9-foot (2.7 m) SpongeBob inflatable figures. The film was a box office success and grossed $85 million in the United States and $140 million worldwide,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup> and received generally positive reviews from critics. A <a href="/wiki/Sequel#Stand-alone_sequels" title="Sequel">stand-alone sequel</a> titled <i><a href="/wiki/The_SpongeBob_Movie:_Sponge_Out_of_Water" title="The SpongeBob Movie: Sponge Out of Water">The SpongeBob Movie: Sponge Out of Water</a></i> was released on February 6, 2015, and a second sequel is speculated to be released in 2019.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (January 2017)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> The film marks the fourth film made by Nickelodeon Movies to be based on a Nicktoon.</p>
<p></p>

<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-20"><a href="#References"><span class="tocnumber">8</span> <span class="toctext">References</span></a></li>

</div>
<p></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Plot">Plot</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=The_SpongeBob_SquarePants_Movie&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Plot">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>A group of pirates find tickets to watch <i>The SpongeBob Movie</i> in a treasure chest and enthusiastically sing the <i>SpongeBob SquarePants</i> theme song, enter a movie theater, raid it and sit down to watch the movie.</p>
<p>The film opens with SpongeBob Squarepants dreaming about managing the <a href="/wiki/Krusty_Krab" title="Krusty Krab">Krusty Krab</a> restaurant and saving the day during a crisis. He wakes up and cheerfully prepares for the opening ceremony for The Krusty Krab 2, expecting his boss Mr. Krabs to promote him to manager of the new restaurant. However, Krabs instead names Squidward Tentacles manager, believing SpongeBob is too immature to handle the role.</p>
<p>That night, SpongeBob goes to his favorite restaurant, Goofy Goober's, where drowns his sorrows in ice cream with his best friend Patrick Star. Elsewhere, Mr. Krabs' business rival Plankton steals King Neptune's crown, leaving evidence false evidence to frame Mr. Krabs for the crime, and sends the crown to Shell City, a distant, mysterious land from which no fish has returned. The next morning, Neptune barges into the Krusty Krab 2 and threatens Mr. Krabs for his alleged thievery. SpongeBob later arrives and chastises Krabs under the influence of an <a href="/wiki/Ice_cream_headache" title="Ice cream headache">ice cream headache</a>, but seeing his boss's life is at risk, he promises Neptune that he will retrieve the crown from Shell City. Neptune freezes Krabs and orders SpongeBob to return with the crown in six days for him to spare Krabs' life. Neptune's sympathetic daughter, Princess Mindy, gives Spongebob a Bag of Winds so that they can return from Shell City once they find the crown. SpongeBob and Patrick leave for Shell City in the Patty Wagon, a car shaped like a Krabby Patty.</p>
<p>After Spongebob and Patrick leave, Plankton steals the Krabby Patty formula and uses it to produce and sell Krabby Patties at his restaurant, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chum_Bucket" title="Chum Bucket">Chum Bucket</a>, claiming that Krabs bequeathed him the recipe. As a contingency, he hires a hitman named Dennis to eliminate SpongeBob and Patrick. Squidward discovers the truth about Plankton stealing Neptune's crown and tries to alert Neptune. However, Plankton uses mind-controlling bucket helmets, disguised as souvenirs, to control Bikini Bottom's residents, including Squidward, and renames the city Planktopolis.</p>
<p>As their journey continues, SpongeBob and Patrick reach a dangerous trench, but Mindy helps them past it by making them think she can turn them into men. They are stopped by Dennis, who tries to crush them with his spiked boots, but he is in turn stepped on by a seemingly massive <a href="/wiki/Standard_diving_dress" title="Standard diving dress">hardhat diver</a> they believe to be a <a href="/wiki/Cyclops" title="Cyclops">Cyclops</a>. The diver grabs SpongeBob and Patrick, and takes them to his beachside store, revealed to be Shell City. At the store, SpongeBob and Patrick find the crown, but are nearly killed when the diver attempts to dry them out using a heat lamp. Their tears short-circuit the lamp's power cord, and its smoke activates the sprinkler system, reviving their bodies and the other dried sea creatures intended to be sold as souvenirs. As the sea creatures attack the diver, SpongeBob and Patrick take the crown and head for the beach. Patrick inadvertently loses the Bag of Winds while attempting to use it, but <a href="/wiki/David_Hasselhoff" title="David Hasselhoff">David Hasselhoff</a> appears and offers them a ride; Dennis catches up to them but is knocked by a <a href="/wiki/Catamaran" title="Catamaran">catamaran</a> back into the sea.</p>
<p>At the Krusty Krab 2, King Neptune arrives to execute Mr. Krabs. SpongeBob and Patrick return with the crown just in time and confront Plankton, who drops a mind-control bucket on Neptune, enslaving him. SpongeBob performs the song "Goofy Goober Rock" and transforms into an <a href="/wiki/Electric_guitar" title="Electric guitar">electric guitar</a>-wielding wizard, freeing Neptune and Bikini Bottom's residents during of the song. Plankton is arrested, and Neptune thanks SpongeBob for his bravery and thaws Mr. Krabs, who makes SpongeBob manager of the Krusty Krab 2 in gratitude.</p>
<p>A post-credits scene shows a theater usher telling the pirates to leave the theater so she can clean up the mess they left, to which the pirates reluctantly agree.</p>
