<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Video_game">Video game</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=The_SpongeBob_SquarePants_Movie&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Video game">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/The_SpongeBob_SquarePants_Movie_(video_game)" title="The SpongeBob SquarePants Movie (video game)">The SpongeBob SquarePants Movie (video game)</a></div>
<p>A <a href="/wiki/The_SpongeBob_SquarePants_Movie_(video_game)" title="The SpongeBob SquarePants Movie (video game)">video game</a> based on the film was released for <a href="/wiki/PlayStation_2" title="PlayStation 2">PlayStation 2</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-150"><a href="#cite_note-150">[150]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Microsoft_Windows" title="Microsoft Windows">PC</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-151"><a href="#cite_note-151">[151]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Game_Boy_Advance" title="Game Boy Advance">Game Boy Advance</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-GBA_152-0"><a href="#cite_note-GBA-152">[152]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Xbox_(console)" title="Xbox (console)">Xbox</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-153"><a href="#cite_note-153">[153]</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/GameCube" title="GameCube">GameCube</a> on October 27, 2004<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-154"><a href="#cite_note-154">[154]</a></sup> for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/OS_X" title="OS X">Mac OS X</a> in 2005<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-155"><a href="#cite_note-155">[155]</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/PlayStation_3" title="PlayStation 3">PlayStation 3</a> on February 7, 2012.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-156"><a href="#cite_note-156">[156]</a></sup> The home-console version was developed by <a href="/wiki/Heavy_Iron_Studios" title="Heavy Iron Studios">Heavy Iron Studios</a>;<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-VG_157-0"><a href="#cite_note-VG-157">[157]</a></sup> the Game Boy Advance version was developed by <a href="/wiki/WayForward_Technologies" title="WayForward Technologies">WayForward Technologies</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-GBA_152-1"><a href="#cite_note-GBA-152">[152]</a></sup> and published by <a href="/wiki/THQ" title="THQ">THQ</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-158"><a href="#cite_note-158">[158]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-159"><a href="#cite_note-159">[159]</a></sup></p>
<p>It was created on the same engine as <i><a href="/wiki/SpongeBob_SquarePants:_Battle_for_Bikini_Bottom" title="SpongeBob SquarePants: Battle for Bikini Bottom">SpongeBob SquarePants: Battle for Bikini Bottom</a></i>. Game developer Heavy Iron Studios tweaked the graphics to give the game a sharper and more-imaginative look than <i>Battle for Bikini Bottom</i>. It increased the polygon count, added several racing levels and incorporated many creatures from the film.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-VG_157-1"><a href="#cite_note-VG-157">[157]</a></sup> The game's plot was based on the film, with SpongeBob and Patrick on a mission taking them outside Bikini Bottom to retrieve Neptune's crown.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-160"><a href="#cite_note-160">[160]</a></sup> On October 4, 2004, THQ announced the game's <a href="/wiki/Mobile_phone" title="Mobile phone">mobile</a> release.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Mobile_161-0"><a href="#cite_note-Mobile-161">[161]</a></sup> Nickelodeon vice-president for new-media business development Paul Jelinek said, "As one of the leading publishers of wireless entertainment content, THQ Wireless is introducing the SpongeBob SquarePants license to a whole new audience of gamers [...] THQ has been a great partner to Nickelodeon over the years and we look forward to the same standard of excellence with these upcoming SpongeBob SquarePants games for wireless devices."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Mobile_161-1"><a href="#cite_note-Mobile-161">[161]</a></sup> The mobile console was developed by Amplified Games.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-162"><a href="#cite_note-162">[162]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sequels">Sequels</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=The_SpongeBob_SquarePants_Movie&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Sequels">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/The_SpongeBob_Movie:_Sponge_Out_of_Water" title="The SpongeBob Movie: Sponge Out of Water">The SpongeBob Movie: Sponge Out of Water</a></div>
<p>On February 28, 2012, the production of a <a href="/wiki/The_SpongeBob_Movie:_Sponge_Out_of_Water" title="The SpongeBob Movie: Sponge Out of Water">sequel</a> was announced; it would be directed by <a href="/wiki/Paul_Tibbitt" title="Paul Tibbitt">Paul Tibbitt</a>, written by <a href="/wiki/Jonathan_Aibel_and_Glenn_Berger" title="Jonathan Aibel and Glenn Berger">Jonathan Aibel and Glenn Berger</a> and produced by Stephen Hillenburg<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Var1_163-0"><a href="#cite_note-Var1-163">[163]</a></sup> for a late-2014 release.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-164"><a href="#cite_note-164">[164]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-HollyWood_165-0"><a href="#cite_note-HollyWood-165">[165]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-166"><a href="#cite_note-166">[166]</a></sup> On August 1, 2013, Paramount changed the sequel's release date to February 13, 2015.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-hollywoodreporter1_167-0"><a href="#cite_note-hollywoodreporter1-167">[167]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-168"><a href="#cite_note-168">[168]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-169"><a href="#cite_note-169">[169]</a></sup> It was announced in early June 2014 that the film would instead be released on February 6, 2015, to avoid competition with <a href="/wiki/Universal_Studios" title="Universal Studios">Universal Pictures</a>' <i><a href="/wiki/Fifty_Shades_of_Grey_(film)" title="Fifty Shades of Grey (film)">Fifty Shades of Grey</a></i>, which was set for a February 13, 2015 release.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-170"><a href="#cite_note-170">[170]</a></sup> A third film has been announced and has a release date of February 8, 2019.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-171"><a href="#cite_note-171">[171]</a></sup></p>
